hindu parampara main paanch tatwon par vishesh jor diya gaya he
 We see part of God in earth, water, fire, sky and air
 in paanchon tatwon main agni ko sabase zyada pavitra mana jaataa he
 The lamp is considered most valuable and sacred as a symbol of fire
 deepak kaa mahatv itnaa zyada he ki ,ham deepon kaa ek puraa parv "deepawali" bhi manaate hai
 We consider God as the Light
 atah deepak jalaakar uski jyoti ke rup main ishwar kaa dhyaan karte hai
 a lamp concentrates the mind and a prayer with a concentrated mind is approved
 karthik kaa maheenaa dipadaan ke liye vishesh hota he
 In this month, by lighting lamps of different faces, we can fulfill our different desires
 ek mukhi deepaksaamanya rup se har puja paath or mantra jaap ke purv ek mukhi deepak jalaayaa jaataa he
 There are two things in this lamp, out of which only one end is lit
 is tarah ke deepak ko jalaakar koi bhi puja upasna kii ja sakati he
 By lighting such a lamp one can easily find the grace of God
 ye deepak puure karthik maah main tulsi ke paudhe ke neeche jalaayaa jaataa haido mukhi deepakado mukhi deepak saamaanya rup se nahin jalaayaa jaataa
 This lamp is used for health and lifesaving
 is tarah ke deepak main bhi do batiyaan hoti hai , jisame do sire jalaae jate hai
 In Kartik month, light two face lamps in front of Lord Shiva
 Doing this will protect you from age and health problems
 Keep in mind that the lamp should be of ghee
 teen mukhi deepakatin mukhi deepak vishesh dashaon main khub laabhakaari hota he
 Burning such lamps removes the problem of enemy obstruction and opponents
 is tarah ke deepak main bhi do batiyaan hoti hai or teen sire jalaae jate hai
 Filling mustard oil in this lamp will benefit quickly
 chaar mukhi deepakahar tarah kii vishesh kaamanaayon kii purti ke liye chaar mukhi deepak jalaayaa jaataa he
 This lamp is used most for getting wealth, planetary dosha and for attaining accomplishment
 is tarah ke deepak main do batiyaan hoti hai or chaaron sire jalaae jate hai
 This type of lamp is lit at the main place of worship and the larger it is, the better
 is baat kaa jarur khyaal rakhen ki deepak main ghi hi bharaa jayega
 If this lamp is lit daily in front of Maa Lakshmi in Kartik month, then money-related problems are overcome
 Six Mukhi lamps are lit for the attainment of six-faced lamp and for the prevention of child related problems
 is tarah ke deepak main teen batiyaan hoti hai or in baatiyon ke chah siron ko jalaayaa jaataa he
 If the husband and wife light this lamp together then the problems related to the child are easily solved
 jin dampattiyon ko santan sambandhi koi samasya he wo ganesh ji ke saamne chah mukhi deepak jalaaen

 magar, congress ko ab tak is disha main koi bada netritv haath nahin laga he

 Russian tennis tennis player Sharapova criticized the media for failing to distort the facts related to the news of her failing a doping test and presenting a correct report about it

 The sports world is shocked after hearing this news
 diggaj tennis khilaadi ne fasebuk par apane prashansakon ko ek post ke jariye shanivaar ko bataaya ki vah bahut abhaari hai, jis prakaar se unke prashansakon ne un par apana bharosa jataayaa or samarthan diya
 He posted, "I know that there are some, not all, but some people in the media who have failed to present the actual report related to the doping case
" " Sharapova further wrote in her post, "one report states that i was warned five times about 'meldron', which is not true and has never happened
" " The tennis player further wrote, "I did not know about the ban, i will not give any reason for this
 maine 22 disambar, 2015 main mili i-mail ke bare main aapako pehle hi bataaya tha
 i should have paid more attention to it
 " It is noteworthy that Sharapova was consuming the drug 'meldonium' (also known as 'mildronate') for the last 10 years due to health problems, which was included in the list of drugs banned by WADA from January 1, 2016

 tirthraj prayag kaa ullekh dharamshastron main bhi miltaa he
 It is said that this is the place from where Kewat crossed the Ganges to Lord Rama

 Kumbh Mela is held at four places
 haridwar, prayag, nasik or ujjain main kumbh kaa mela hota he
 At these four places, Kumbh is organized every 3 years, hence Kumbh is held only after 12 years at any one place
 shastron main bhi he kumbh kaa zikrakumbh meley kaa varnan shastron main miltaa he
 It is said that this festival is related to ocean churning
 isse judi ek puranic katha bhi he

 devtaa-asur jab amrit kalash ko ek duusare se chin rah the, tab uski kuch boonden dharti kii teen nadiyon main giri thim

 jahaan ye boonden giri thim, us sthaan par kumbh kaa aayojan hota he

 ab sawaal ye bhi he ki kumbh or ardh kumbh main kya antar he
 What is Ardh Kumbh? Ardhkumbh is organized in Haridwar and Prayag in a gap of 6 years between two Kumbh festivals
 puranic granthon main bhi kumbh evam ardh kumbh ke aayojan ko lekar jyotishiya vishleshan hai
 Kumbh festival starts from Haridwar at an interval of every 3 years
 haridwar ke baad kumbh parv prayag nasik or ujjain main manaaya jaataa he
 There is a difference of 3 years between the Kumbh festival celebrated in Prayag and Haridwar and the Kumbha festival celebrated in Prayag and Nashik
 yahaan magh mela sangam par yojit ek vaarshik samaaroh he
 Kumbh festival is a highly revered festival of Hinduism in which crores of devotees take bath in Haridwar, Prayag, Ujjain and Nashik places of Kumbh festival
 shastron ke mutabik, chaar vishesh sthanon par hi kumbh mela lag saktaa he

 inamen se prayek sthaan par har 12wein saal main, haridwar or prayag main do kumbh parvon ke bich chah saal ke antaraal main ardhakumbh bhi hota he

 amrit kalash ko swarglok tak le jane main jayant ko 12 din lage

 isiilie taron ke kram ke anusaar har 12wein varsh kumbh parv vibhinn tirth sthanon par yojit hota he

 amrit kii bunde chhalakane ke samay jin raashiyon main surya, chandramaa, brihaspati kii sthiti ke vishisht yoga ke avasar rahete hai
 There, the festival of Kumbh is organized in these zodiac signs on the basis of houses
 is amrit kalash kii raksha main surya, guru or chandramaa ke vishesh praytn rahe the

what is the shaharon kii gandagi lekar girte in naalon ne hamaari nadiyon kaa kya haal kiya he, aap chahen to kisi bhi shahar se guzarane vaali kisi bhi nadi ko dekh sakate hai
 Sewage treatment is an expensive medium
 ise lagaana or iskaa rakrakhaav donon
 In many cities of India, sewage of a large part of the population does not fall in any drain
 jagah-jagah naale bajabajate mil jaaenge
 On 14 July, 4 people died while cleaning sewer in Delhi's Githorni, the same day the Madras High Court ordered the Central and State Government to ban employment as a scavenger and Section 7 of their Rehabilitation Act 2013
 Under it, there is a ban on employing people for employment or such works for the fatal cleaning of drains and septic tanks
 1 janvari, 2014 se 20 march, 2017 ke bich tamilnadu main sir par mailaa dhone ke kaaran 30 safaikamiyon kii maut ho chuki he
 These deaths can be prevented only when people stop going to sewer and septic tanks
 akhir gater, siver yaa manhole saaf karne ke liye asthai karmchaariyon ko hi kyon rakhaa jaataa he
 Does the system know that death is fixed at some point in this work
 isliye agar pakki naukari hogi to uski jagah par parivaar ke kisi sadsy ko rakhana padegaa
 During research, it was revealed that in any municipality, while cleaning sewer or gutter, accurate statistics of death due to suffocation are not maintained
 janvari, 2015 main brihanmumbai nagarpalika ne bataaya tha ki pichley chah saal main yani 2009 se 2015 ke bich 1386 safaikarmiyon kii maut ho gai he or yah sankhya badhati hi ja rahi he
 There are 35,000 scavengers in Mumbai, most of whom are hired on contract
 2014 main supreme court ne aadesh diya tha ki naaliyon kii safai ke dauraan maare gaye karmchaariyon ke parivaar waalon ko das lakh rupee die jaaenge
 But many reports found that the relatives of the scavengers who died did not get compensation
 12 july, 2011 ko supreme court ne ek aitihaasik aadesh diya jisamen sir par mailaa dhone vaale mazaduron or sivej kamgaaron kii durdasha ko rekhaankit kiya gaya
 The court also strongly criticized the government's insensitivity to their welfare and safety
 supreme court ne maare gaye logon ke pariwaron ko zyaada muawza dene kaa aadesh to diya hi saath hi shahari nikaayon ko turant dilli hycourt ke us aadesh kaa paalan karne kaa nirdesh diya jisamen sivej main kaam karne waalon kii suraksha sunishchit karne kii baat kahi gai thi
 In 2007 Human Rights Law Network, an NGO, filed a PIL in the Delhi High Court
 ye sanstha dilli ke hazaron mailaa dhone vaale mazaduron kii pratinidhi he jo dilli jal board, emsidi, endiemasi, disidisi, seepidblyoody main kaam karte hai
 Hearing the petition of the NGO, the High Court also admitted that the situation was serious
 yachika main in maamalon kaa zikr kiya gaya or dilli hycourt ne mana ki halaat kaafii gambhir hai
 The court immediately ordered all local bodies to provide free medical facilities and compensation to the sewage workers
 iske alaava apane kaam se judi bimariyon se jujh rahe sivej mazdooron ko muawza, unki maut ke baad unke ashriton ko pief or duusari suvidhaayen dene kii baat kahi

 between 2009 and 2015 and this number is increasing

 magar kai report main is baat kaa zikr mila ki marane vaale safaikarmiyon ke parijanon ko muawza nahin miltaa he
 On July 12, 2011, the Supreme Court passed a landmark order outlining the plight of manual scavengers and sewage workers
 court ne unke kalyaan or suraksha ko lekar sarkaar kii samvedanheenata kii bhi kadi aalochana kii
 Not only did the Supreme Court order more compensation to the families of those killed, as well as directing the urban bodies to immediately follow the Delhi High Court's order that ensures the safety of those working in sewage
 2007 main ek enjio Human Rights Law Network ne dilli hycourt main ek janhit yachika daayar kii
 These organizations are representative of thousands of manual scavengers of Delhi who work in Delhi Jal Board, MCD, NDMC, DSIDC, CPWD

 "the date, time and geolocation coordinates appear in the aviation details seen on the video

 saal 2016 vaale footage main flite data maujuud nahin tha, haalanki puure video par vahi band najar aayaa jis par likhaa tha "ektual footage of detected indian sabamarine
 "both in 2016 and 2019, Pakistan showed only a 43-second short video featuring a similar band
